<div class="facility-about-and-photos-wrapper">
<section class="facility-about facility-details">
<h3 class="section-heading">
<span class="heading-text">
About <span class="facility-name">Advantage Storage - Rowlett East</span>
</span>
</h3>
<div class="facility-description-wrapper">
<p class="facility-description">Advantage Storage at 7301 Lakeview Parkway (aka HWY 66) is located in Rowlett (servicing Rowlett areas). We are offering a safe, clean and state-of-the-art facility for all your storage needs, whether for personal or business space.<br/>
<br/>
We offer climate-controlled as well as standard, drive-up storage units, with all of our units at ground level. Carts and dollies are also available for use while on site. Advantage Storage offers inexpensive, secure, self-storage. Storage units meet a variety of needs:<br/>
<br/>
While Moving, Building or Selling your Home<br/>
<br/>
To Free Valuable Living and Garage Space<br/>
<br/>
Offsite Storage for Rarely Used Items<br/>
<br/>
We protect your valuable property with the best in security measures, including a code access gate and 24-hour camera surveillance. Our managers do strive to maintain an active presence on the property. We also maintain an ongoing pest control program performed monthly by a professional pest control company.<br/>
<br/>
Come on down to see all that we offer, and don't forget to ask about our move-in specials!</p>
<a href="#" class="read-more-toggle facility-learn-more">
<span class="more">Read more</span>
<span class="less">Read less</span>
<i class="icon icon--dropdown"></i>
</a>
</div>
</section>

<div class="how-it-works__steps">
<div class="how-it-works-step">
<img src="//www.static-selfstorage.com/images/select-unit.10054127.svg" data-pagespeed-url-hash="2931976970" onload="pagespeed.CriticalImages.checkImageForCriticality(this);" data-pagespeed-lsc-url="https://www.static-selfstorage.com/images/select-unit.10054127.svg">

1. Select your unit
</div>
</div>
<div class="how-it-works-step">
<img src="//www.static-selfstorage.com/images/reserve-for-free.10054127.svg" data-pagespeed-url-hash="2454487500" onload="pagespeed.CriticalImages.checkImageForCriticality(this);" data-pagespeed-lsc-url="https://www.static-selfstorage.com/images/reserve-for-free.10054127.svg">
<div class="step-text">
2. Reserve for free
</div>
<div class="step-subtext">
Cancel or change your reservation at any time, risk-free
</div>
</div>
<div class="how-it-works-step">
<img src="//www.static-selfstorage.com/images/visit-facility.10054127.svg" data-pagespeed-url-hash="1577672532" onload="pagespeed.CriticalImages.checkImageForCriticality(this);" data-pagespeed-lsc-url="https://www.static-selfstorage.com/images/visit-facility.10054127.svg">
<div class="step-text">
3. Visit your facility
</div>
</div>
<div class="how-it-works-step">

</div>

<div id="modal--wte--amenities" class="modal fade">
<div class="modal-dialog" role="document">
<div class="modal-header">
<button type="button" class="close" data-dismiss="modal" aria-label="Close">
<span aria-hidden="true">&times;</span>
</button>
<h4 class="modal-title">Amenities Guide</h4>
</div>
<div class="modal-body">
<div class="card">
<div class="card-block">
<img class="unit-amenity__image" data-src="//www.static-selfstorage.com/images/wte-icon--climate-control.10054127.png" alt=""/>
<h4 class="unit-amenity__title">Climate Control</h4>
<p class="unit-amenity__description">The facility will maintain a safe temperature and humidity level for your unit. If youâre storing something temperature-sensitive or particularly valuable, climate control is a good idea.</p>
</div>
</div>
<div class="card">
<div class="card-block">
<img class="unit-amenity__image" data-src="//www.static-selfstorage.com/images/wte-icon--drive-up-access.10054127.png" alt=""/>
<h4 class="unit-amenity__title">Drive-Up Access</h4>
<p class="unit-amenity__description">You can pull your moving truck or vehicle right up to the unit. This is rarely available for indoor units.</p>
</div>
</div>
<div class="card">
<div class="card-block">
<img class="unit-amenity__image" data-src="//www.static-selfstorage.com/images/wte-icon--truck-rental.10054127.png" alt=""/>
<h4 class="unit-amenity__title">Truck Rental</h4>
<p class="unit-amenity__description">Some facilities will let you rent their moving truck for free. Specific terms and restrictions will vary by facility (e.g., mileage limits, time limits, insurance requirements, refueling protocol).</p>
</div>
</div>
<div class="card">
<div class="card-block">
<img class="unit-amenity__image" data-src="//www.static-selfstorage.com/images/wte-icon--24-hour-access.10054127.png" alt=""/>
<h4 class="unit-amenity__title">24-Hour Access</h4>
<p class="unit-amenity__description">You have access to your unit at any time. Restrictions may applyâfor example, your facility could require manager approval. Some facilities only allow business customers 24-hour access or may charge additional fees.</p>
</div>
</div>
<div class="card">
<div class="card-block">
<img class="unit-amenity__image" data-src="//www.static-selfstorage.com/images/wte-icon--locks.10054127.png" alt=""/>
<h4 class="unit-amenity__title">Locks</h4>
<p class="unit-amenity__description">Most facilities require you to bring your own lock, although many will sell locks onsite. We recommend closed-shackle padlocks, disc locks or cylinder locks. Standard or combination padlocks are easily picked and not recommended.</p>
</div>
</div>
<div class="card">
<div class="card-block">
<img class="unit-amenity__image" data-src="//www.static-selfstorage.com/images/wte-icon--security.10054127.png" alt=""/>
<h4 class="unit-amenity__title">Security</h4>
<p class="unit-amenity__description">Video camera surveillance, electronic gates and âfenced + lightedâ can all increase the security of the facility. A manager who lives onsite means that someone will be on the premises during non-business hours.</p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>

<div id="modal--review-drawing" class="modal fade" tabindex="-1" role="dialog" aria-labelledby="modal--review-drawing__heading" aria-hidden="true">

<div class="modal-content">
<div class="modal-header">
<button class="close" data-dismiss="modal">&#215;</button>
<h4 class="modal-title" id="modal--review-drawing__heading">Renter Reviews: Amazon Gift Card Drawing</h4>
</div>
<div class="modal-body">
<h4>Terms &amp; Conditions</h4>
<p>On the first business day of every month, we randomly select one storage customer who left a review on SpareFoot during the previous month.
We email this customer at the address provided with their review, letting them know they have won our drawing for a $250 Amazon gift card.
Our email states that the customer has 7 days to reply and verify their preferred email address for electronic delivery of the gift card.
If they reply in time, the customer will receive a $250 Amazon gift card, delivered electronically to their preferred email address within
1 business day. If the customer does not reply in time, we go back and randomly select a different storage customer, and this process
repeats until we have a verified winner.</p>
<h4>Eligibility</h4>
<p>Every customer who submits a storage review with valid email address will be automatically entered into the Renter Reviews: Amazon Gift
Card Drawing. Eligibility is dependent on your providing a valid email address in the review submission form of this page.</p>
</div>

<a data-dismiss="modal" class="button button--primary">Close</a>

<div id="modal--vehicle-size-guide" class="modal fade search-modal" role="dialog">
<div class="modal-dialog" role="document">
<div class="modal-content">
<div class="modal-header">
<h4 class="modal-title">Vehicle Unit Size Guide</h4>
<button type="button" class="close" data-dismiss="modal" aria-label="Close">
<span aria-hidden="true">&times;</span>
</button>
</div>
<div class="modal-body">
<div>
<h4 class="search-modal-content-header">15' Long</h4>
<p class="search-modal-content-description">Most coupes, hatchbacks, crossovers and small SUVs that come under 15 feet in length will fit. If you choose this size, you might be left with only a few inches of space.</p>
</div>
<div>
<h4 class="search-modal-content-header">20' Long</h4>
<p class="search-modal-content-description">Most cars will fit comfortably, including SUVs, crossovers, sedans, minivans, pickup trucks and most full-sized vans.</p>
</div>
<div>
<h4 class="search-modal-content-header">25' Long</h4>
<p class="search-modal-content-description">Perfect for larger vehicles or a boat. Small Class B campers, small Class C campers, travel trailers, toy trailers and pop-ups may also fit in spaces designed for RV storage.</p>
</div>
<div>
<h4 class="search-modal-content-header">30' Long</h4>
<p class="search-modal-content-description">Store one or multiple vehicles with plenty of other possessions, including furniture and large appliances. This size can also handle smaller-to-medium sized Class B campers and travel trailers, large pop-ups, and smaller Class C campers and fifth-wheel trailers.</p>
</div>
<div>
<h4 class="search-modal-content-header">35' Long</h4>
<p class="search-modal-content-description">Store one or multiple vehicles with plenty of other possessions, including furniture and large appliances. This size can typically contain large Class B and Class C campers, mid-to-large sized travel trailers, small-to-mid sized fifth-wheel campers, large toy trailers, and small Class A campers.</p>
</div>
<div>
<h4 class="search-modal-content-header">40' Long</h4>
<p class="search-modal-content-description">All but the largest of RVs will fit into a 40' storage space. This includes most Class A campers, large travel trailers and fifth-wheel trailers. Remember that with the added length often comes additional width and height, meaning that many of these extra-large vehicles will require ceilings with a minimum height of 15 feet.</p>
</div>
<div>
<h4 class="search-modal-content-header">50' Long</h4>
<p class="search-modal-content-description">50' RV storage space will handle the largest of RVs, like large Class A campers, travel trailers and destination trailers. Remember that with the added length often comes additional width and height, meaning that many of these extra-large vehicles will require ceilings with a minimum height of 15 feet.</p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div id="modal--vehicle-accommodations-guide" class="modal fade search-modal" role="dialog">
<div class="modal-dialog" role="document">
<div class="modal-content">
<div class="modal-header">
<h4 class="modal-title">Vehicle Accommodations Guide</h4>
<button type="button" class="close" data-dismiss="modal" aria-label="Close">
<span aria-hidden="true">&times;</span>
</button>
</div>
<div class="modal-body">
<div>
<h4 class="search-modal-content-header">Outdoor Uncovered Unit</h4>
<p class="search-modal-content-description">A Vehicle Parking Space is exactly what it sounds like: an area for you to park your vehicle. The parking area may be paved or on a variety of unpaved surfaces including gravel, dirt, or an open field on the storage facilityâs grounds.</p>
</div>
<div>
<h4 class="search-modal-content-header">Outdoor Covered Unit</h4>
<p class="search-modal-content-description">With Covered vehicle storage, youâll typically park your vehicle under a standalone roof alongside other vehicles, though some covered units do have three walls separating your vehicle from the rest. Though you wonât get as much protection as from an enclosed unit or indoor, the roof structure will protect your vehicle from the harshest elements.</p>
</div>
<div>
<h4 class="search-modal-content-header">Indoor Unit</h4>
<p class="search-modal-content-description">With Indoor vehicle storage, your vehicle will be parked inside a large structure such as a warehouse with other vehicles. Indoor vehicle storage provides the same protection from the elements as enclosed storage, but since your vehicle will be in a shared space there may be different access requirements.</p>
</div>
<div>
<h4 class="search-modal-content-header">Enclosed Unit</h4>
<p class="search-modal-content-description">Enclosed Vehicle Storage is the safest and most secure means of storing your vehicle. These are large self-storage units that essentially act as garages you can drive your vehicle straight into, and are accessed via a large roll-up door. Enclosed units provide protection from winter weather and prevent any unwanted access to your vehicle.</p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>

<h4 class="body-header">Terms & conditions</h4>
<h5 class="body-section-header">SelfStorage.com Move-in Rebate Details</h5>
<div class="paragraph">
Certain facilities and units at SelfStorage.com are eligible for a $25 Visa Gift Card Rebate when you book
a unit through SelfStorage.com or one of its partner sites and subsequently move into the booked unit. Any
units or facilities eligible for a Move-in Rebate will be clearly marked on our site. Facilities and
units that do not have Move-in Rebate eligible badging are not eligible for move-in rebate claims
unless specifically offered on a phone call with SelfStorage.com or one of its partner sites where the
customer made a storage reservation.
</div>
<h5 class="body-section-header">You must move into the facility that you booked on SelfStorage.com</h5>
<div class="paragraph">
You must move into the facility that you booked with SelfStorage.com in accordance with the move-in date
specified in your confirmed booking or a compatible date to be eligible to receive the move-in
rebate. Your rebate will be processed within 5-7 business days of submission. All move-in rebates
must be claimed within 30 days of moving into the unit.
</div>
<h5 class="body-section-header">Notifying SelfStorage.com of a Claim</h5>
<div class="paragraph">
You must file a rebate claim form within thirty (30) days after you moved into the unit booked
through SelfStorage.com, its partner sites, or its call center.
</div>
<h5 class="body-section-header">Verification of Claims and Method of Payment</h5>
<div class="paragraph">
The $25 Visa Gift Card Move-in Rebate will be sent in the form of a digital gift card to the email
address provided on the claims form. You must provide SelfStorage.com a digital copy of the lease or
receipt proving that you moved into the facility in order to qualify for the rebate. Digital gift
cards are subject to availability and may be substituted for alternative gift cards for eligible
claims. Move-in Rebate claims can be nullified if the confirmation code, name or email address
provided do not match a reservation or move-in in the SelfStorage.com system.
</div>
<h5 class="body-section-header">Limit</h5>
<div class="paragraph">
One (1) move-in offer of $25.00 (USD) per customer per year. Visa Prepaid Card is issued by The
Bancorp Bank, Member FDIC, pursuant to licenses from VisaÂ® U.S.A., Inc. Due to varying local laws,
the gift card amount you receive will be for the specified amount minus any discounts or promotions.
Taxes and fees are not refundable.
</div>

<div id="modal--vehicle-size-guide" class="modal fade search-modal" role="dialog">
<div class="modal-dialog" role="document">
<div class="modal-content">
<div class="modal-header">
<h4 class="modal-title">Vehicle Unit Size Guide</h4>
<button type="button" class="close" data-dismiss="modal" aria-label="Close">
<span aria-hidden="true">&times;</span>
</button>
</div>
<div class="modal-body">
<div>
<h4 class="search-modal-content-header">15' Long</h4>
<p class="search-modal-content-description">Most coupes, hatchbacks, crossovers and small SUVs that come under 15 feet in length will fit. If you choose this size, you might be left with only a few inches of space.</p>
</div>
<div>
<h4 class="search-modal-content-header">20' Long</h4>
<p class="search-modal-content-description">Most cars will fit comfortably, including SUVs, crossovers, sedans, minivans, pickup trucks and most full-sized vans.</p>
</div>
<div>
<h4 class="search-modal-content-header">25' Long</h4>
<p class="search-modal-content-description">Perfect for larger vehicles or a boat. Small Class B campers, small Class C campers, travel trailers, toy trailers and pop-ups may also fit in spaces designed for RV storage.</p>
</div>
<div>
<h4 class="search-modal-content-header">30' Long</h4>
<p class="search-modal-content-description">Store one or multiple vehicles with plenty of other possessions, including furniture and large appliances. This size can also handle smaller-to-medium sized Class B campers and travel trailers, large pop-ups, and smaller Class C campers and fifth-wheel trailers.</p>
</div>
<div>
<h4 class="search-modal-content-header">35' Long</h4>
<p class="search-modal-content-description">Store one or multiple vehicles with plenty of other possessions, including furniture and large appliances. This size can typically contain large Class B and Class C campers, mid-to-large sized travel trailers, small-to-mid sized fifth-wheel campers, large toy trailers, and small Class A campers.</p>
</div>
<div>
<h4 class="search-modal-content-header">40' Long</h4>
<p class="search-modal-content-description">All but the largest of RVs will fit into a 40' storage space. This includes most Class A campers, large travel trailers and fifth-wheel trailers. Remember that with the added length often comes additional width and height, meaning that many of these extra-large vehicles will require ceilings with a minimum height of 15 feet.</p>
</div>
<div>
<h4 class="search-modal-content-header">50' Long</h4>
<p class="search-modal-content-description">50' RV storage space will handle the largest of RVs, like large Class A campers, travel trailers and destination trailers. Remember that with the added length often comes additional width and height, meaning that many of these extra-large vehicles will require ceilings with a minimum height of 15 feet.</p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div id="modal--vehicle-accommodations-guide" class="modal fade search-modal" role="dialog">
<div class="modal-dialog" role="document">
<div class="modal-content">
<div class="modal-header">
<h4 class="modal-title">Vehicle Accommodations Guide</h4>
<button type="button" class="close" data-dismiss="modal" aria-label="Close">
<span aria-hidden="true">&times;</span>
</button>
</div>
<div class="modal-body">
<div>
<h4 class="search-modal-content-header">Outdoor Uncovered Unit</h4>
<p class="search-modal-content-description">A Vehicle Parking Space is exactly what it sounds like: an area for you to park your vehicle. The parking area may be paved or on a variety of unpaved surfaces including gravel, dirt, or an open field on the storage facilityâs grounds.</p>
</div>
<div>
<h4 class="search-modal-content-header">Outdoor Covered Unit</h4>
<p class="search-modal-content-description">With Covered vehicle storage, youâll typically park your vehicle under a standalone roof alongside other vehicles, though some covered units do have three walls separating your vehicle from the rest. Though you wonât get as much protection as from an enclosed unit or indoor, the roof structure will protect your vehicle from the harshest elements.</p>
</div>
<div>
<h4 class="search-modal-content-header">Indoor Unit</h4>
<p class="search-modal-content-description">With Indoor vehicle storage, your vehicle will be parked inside a large structure such as a warehouse with other vehicles. Indoor vehicle storage provides the same protection from the elements as enclosed storage, but since your vehicle will be in a shared space there may be different access requirements.</p>
</div>
<div>
<h4 class="search-modal-content-header">Enclosed Unit</h4>
<p class="search-modal-content-description">Enclosed Vehicle Storage is the safest and most secure means of storing your vehicle. These are large self-storage units that essentially act as garages you can drive your vehicle straight into, and are accessed via a large roll-up door. Enclosed units provide protection from winter weather and prevent any unwanted access to your vehicle.</p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div id="modal--visa-incentive-details" class="modal fade search-modal" role="dialog">
<div class="modal-dialog" role="document">
<div class="modal-content">
<div class="modal-header">
<h4 class="modal-title">How it works</h4>
<button type="button" class="close" data-dismiss="modal" aria-label="Close">
<span aria-hidden="true">&times;</span>
</button>
</div>
<div class="modal-body">

<h4 class="body-header">Terms & conditions</h4>
<h5 class="body-section-header">SelfStorage.com Move-in Rebate Details</h5>
<div class="paragraph">
Certain facilities and units at SelfStorage.com are eligible for a $25 Visa Gift Card Rebate when you book
a unit through SelfStorage.com or one of its partner sites and subsequently move into the booked unit. Any
units or facilities eligible for a Move-in Rebate will be clearly marked on our site. Facilities and
units that do not have Move-in Rebate eligible badging are not eligible for move-in rebate claims
unless specifically offered on a phone call with SelfStorage.com or one of its partner sites where the
customer made a storage reservation.
</div>
<h5 class="body-section-header">You must move into the facility that you booked on SelfStorage.com</h5>
<div class="paragraph">
You must move into the facility that you booked with SelfStorage.com in accordance with the move-in date
specified in your confirmed booking or a compatible date to be eligible to receive the move-in
rebate. Your rebate will be processed within 5-7 business days of submission. All move-in rebates
must be claimed within 30 days of moving into the unit.
</div>
<h5 class="body-section-header">Notifying SelfStorage.com of a Claim</h5>
<div class="paragraph">
You must file a rebate claim form within thirty (30) days after you moved into the unit booked
through SelfStorage.com, its partner sites, or its call center.
</div>
<h5 class="body-section-header">Verification of Claims and Method of Payment</h5>
<div class="paragraph">
The $25 Visa Gift Card Move-in Rebate will be sent in the form of a digital gift card to the email
address provided on the claims form. You must provide SelfStorage.com a digital copy of the lease or
receipt proving that you moved into the facility in order to qualify for the rebate. Digital gift
cards are subject to availability and may be substituted for alternative gift cards for eligible
claims. Move-in Rebate claims can be nullified if the confirmation code, name or email address
provided do not match a reservation or move-in in the SelfStorage.com system.
</div>
<h5 class="body-section-header">Limit</h5>
<div class="paragraph">
One (1) move-in offer of $25.00 (USD) per customer per year. Visa Prepaid Card is issued by The
Bancorp Bank, Member FDIC, pursuant to licenses from VisaÂ® U.S.A., Inc. Due to varying local laws,
the gift card amount you receive will be for the specified amount minus any discounts or promotions.
Taxes and fees are not refundable.
</div>

                </a>

                {% endif %}

                       rel="nofollow">{{ i }}</a>
                </li>
            {% endfor %}

                {% set state = 'disabled' %}
                {% set href = '#' %}

                {% set state = '' %}

                    <span itemprop="addressLocality" class="city locality">{{ facility.location.city }}</span>
                    <span itemprop="addressRegion" class="state region">{{ facility.location.state }}</span>
                    <span itemprop="postalCode" class="zip postal-code">{{ facility.location.zip }}</span>
                </span>

                <span class="facility-distance">{{ facility.distance }} miles away</span>
            </div>

            <div class="facility-phone">
                <a class="js-click-to-call ga-segment-track"
                   data-segment-category="{{ renderContext['trackingCategory'] }}"
                   data-segment-label="click-to-call"
                   data-options='{"facilityId": {{ facility.id }} }'>
                    <i class="icon icon--phone"></i>
                    Call to Book
                </a>
            </div>

            {% if facility.reviews.number %}
                <div class="facility-reviews-rating">
                    <div class="facility-reviews-rating__stars">
                        {% for starIterator in [0,1,2,3,4] %}
                            {% if starIterator < facility.reviews.fullStarsLimit %}
                                <span class="icon icon--star"></span>
                            {% elseif starIterator < facility.reviews.halfStarsLimit %}
                                <span class="icon icon--star--half"></span>
                            {% else %}
                                <span class="icon icon--star--empty"></span>
                            {% endif %}
                        {% endfor %}
                    </div>
                    <p class="facility-reviews-rating__review-count">Based on
                        <a class="link--facility link--facility-reviews ga-segment-track"
                           data-segment-category="{{ renderContext['trackingCategory'] }}"
                           data-segment-label="reviews text"
                           data-options='{"facilityId": {{ facility.id }} }'
                           href="{{ facility.url }}#facility-page-user-reviews"
                           target="_parent"
                        >{{ facility.reviews.text }}</a>
                    </p>
                </div>
            {% endif %}
        </div>

        {% if facility.inNetwork and facility.lowestPrice is not empty %}
            <div class="facility-lowest-price">Starting at <a class="link--facility price ga-segment-track"
               data-segment-category="{{ renderContext['trackingCategory'] }}"
               data-segment-label="starting at price"
               data-options='{"facilityId": {{ facility.id }} }'
               href="{{ facility.url }}"
               target="_parent">${{ facility.lowestPrice }}</a></div>
        {% endif %}

        {% if facility.amenities.aaaActive %}
            {# @todo Any way we can use the aaa-block Volt partial here? Maybe convert it to a Twig template? #}
            <a class="aaa-block link--facility ga-segment-track"
               data-segment-category="{{ renderContext['trackingCategory'] }}"
               data-segment-label="aaa badge"
               data-options='{"facilityId": {{ facility.id }} }'
               href="{{ facility.url }}"
               target="_parent"
               data-toggle="popover"
               data-html="true"
               data-container="body"
               data-placement="top"
               data-trigger="hover"
               data-content="<div class='popover--aaa'>AAA members get first month free (prorated if facility bills on 1st of every month) + $20 Amazon gift card with SelfStorage.com. Cannot be combined with any other offer.</div>">
                <img class="aaa-logo" {{ index > 3 ? 'data-' : '' }}src="{{ images['aaa-discounts-rewards'] }}" alt="AAA Discount Rewards logo" />
                <div class="text-bubble">
                    <span class="promo-text">AAA Members: Get your 1st month free + $20 gift card</span>
                </div>
            </a>
        {% else %}
            {% if facility.promo %}
                <div class="facility-promo">
                    <p class="facility-promo__header">Special Offer:</p>
                    <p class="facility-promo__body">{{ facility.promo }}</p>
                </div>
            {% endif %}
        {% endif %}
    </div>

    {% if showUnits %}
        <div class="facility-units">
            {% set actualStackedUnitCount = 0 %}
            {% for unit in facility.units.stackedUnits %}
                <div class="facility-unit">
                    {% if unit.quantity == 0 and unit.quantity is not null %}
                        <div class="unit-description">
                            <p class="unit-size-type scarcity">No <span class="unit-size">{{ unit.size }}</span> Units Available</p>
                        </div>
                    {% else %}
                        {% set actualStackedUnitCount = actualStackedUnitCount + 1 %}
                        <div class="unit-description">
                            <div>
                                <p class="unit-size-type"><span class="unit-size">{{ unit.size }}</span> {{ unit.type }}</p>
                                <p class="unit-amenities" title="{{ unit.amenities|join(', ') }}">{{ unit.amenities|join(', ') }}</p>
                                {% if unit.special is not empty %}
                                    <p class="unit-promo">
                                        {{ unit.special }}
                                    </p>
                                {% endif %}
                                <!-- sf_5199_vehicle_serp -->
                                {% if unit.special is empty %}
                                    <p class="vehicle-accomodation">
                                        {{ unit.vehicleAccommodation }}
                                    </p>
                                {% endif %}
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    {% endif %}

                    {% if unit.quantity > 0 or unit.quantity is null %}
                        <div class="unit-price">
                            <a href="{{ unit.reserveUrl }}"
                               target="_parent"
                               rel="nofollow"
                               class="link--unit-details ga-segment-track"
                               data-segment-category="{{ renderContext['trackingCategory'] }}"
                               data-segment-label="price"
                               data-options='{ "facilityId": {{ facility.id }}, "unitId": "{{ unit.id }}", "unitSize": "{{ unit.width }} x {{ unit.length }}", "unitPrice": "{{ unit.price }}" }'>
                                {% if unit.isOutOfBookingRange %}
                                    <span class="out-of-range">Out of date range</span>
                                    <span class="link--view-anyway">View Anyway</span>
                                {% elseif not facility.isOpenOnMid %}
                                    <span class="out-of-range">Closed on selected date</span>
                                    <span class="link--view-anyway">View Anyway</span>
                                {% else %}
                                    <span class="effective-price">${{ unit.price }}</span>
                                    <span class="icon icon--next"></span>
                                {% endif %}
                            </a>
                        </div>
                    {% endif %}
                </div>
            {% endfor %}

            <a class="link--facility link--view-more-units ga-segment-track"
               data-segment-category="{{ renderContext['trackingCategory'] }}"
               data-segment-label="compare units at this facility"
               data-options='{"facilityId": {{ facility.id }} }'
               href="{{ facility.url }}#units"
               target="_parent">
                Compare <strong>{{ facility.units.unitsAvailable }}</strong> {{ facility.units.moreUnitsText }} &raquo;
            </a>
        </div>
    {% endif %}
</div>
</script>
